                    Nombre completo *
                  </label>
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    name="nombre"
                    required
                    value={formData.nombre}
                    onChange={handleChange}
                    className="w-full px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-transparent"
                    placeholder="Juan Pérez"
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                    Correo electrónico *
                  </label>
                  <input
                    type="email"
                    name="email"
                    required
                    value={formData.email}
                    onChange={handleChange}
                    className="w-full px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-transparent"
                    placeholder="juan@ejemplo.com"
                  />
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="mb-6">
                <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                  Teléfono
                </label>
                <input
                  type="tel"
                  name="telefono"
                  value={formData.telefono}
                  onChange={handleChange}
                  className="w-full px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-transparent"
                  placeholder="55 1234 5678"
                />
              </div>
              <div className="mb-6">
                <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                  Mensaje *
                </label>
                <textarea
                  name="mensaje"
                  required
                  rows={6}
                  value={formData.mensaje}
                  onChange={handleChange}
                  className="w-full px-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-transparent"
                  placeholder="Cuéntanos sobre tu proyecto, duda o sugerencia..."
                />
              </div>
              <button
                type="submit"
                disabled={isSubmitting}
                className="w-full bg-blue-600 text-white py-3 rounded-xl font-semibold hover:bg-blue-700 transition disabled:opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center gap-2"
              >
                {isSubmitting ? (
                  'Enviando...'
                ) : (
                  <>
                    Enviar mensaje <Send className="h-5 w-5" />
                  </>
                )}
              </button>
            </form>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

    completed: <CheckCircle className="h-4 w-4" />,
    bidding: <Briefcase className="h-4 w-4" />
  };

  const navigation = [
    { name: 'Panel principal', icon: Home, id: 'proyectos' },
    { name: 'Mis proyectos', icon: ClipboardList, id: 'proyectos' },
    { name: 'Mensajes', icon: MessageCircle, id: 'mensajes' },
    { name: 'Pagos y presupuestos', icon: CreditCard, id: 'pagos' },
    { name: 'Mi perfil', icon: User, id: 'perfil' },
    { name: 'Configuración', icon: Settings, id: 'configuracion' },
  ];

  const renderContent = () => {
    switch(activeTab) {
      case 'proyectos':
        return (
          <div>
            <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6 flex-wrap gap-4">
              <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">Mis proyectos</h2>
              <Link
                to="/intake/cliente"
                className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-blue-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700 transition"
              >
                <Plus className="h-5 w-5" />
                Nuevo proyecto
              </Link>
            </div>

            {/* Stats */}
            <div className="grid md:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-8">
              <div className="bg-gradient-to-br from-blue-50 to-blue-100 rounded-xl p-4">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-blue-700">{projects.length}</div>
                <div className="text-sm text-blue-600">Proyectos totales</div>
              </div>
              <div className="bg-gradient-to-br from-green-50 to-green-100 rounded-xl p-4">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-700">
                  {projects.filter(p => p.status === 'completed').length}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-green-600">Completados</div>
              </div>
              <div className="bg-gradient-to-br from-yellow-50 to-yellow-100 rounded-xl p-4">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-yellow-700">
                  {projects.filter(p => p.status === 'in_progress').length}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-yellow-600">En progreso</div>
              </div>
              <div className="bg-gradient-to-br from-purple-50 to-purple-100 rounded-xl p-4">
                <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-purple-700">
                  ${projects.reduce((sum, p) => sum + (p.budget || 0), 0).toLocaleString()}
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-purple-600">Inversión total</div>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Projects List */}
            <div className="space-y-4">
              {projects.map((project) => (
                <div key={project.id} className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-gray-100 p-5 hover:shadow-md transition">
                  <div className="flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center justify-between gap-4">
                    <div className="flex-1">
                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                        <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${statusColors[project.status]}`}>
                          {statusIcons[project.status]}
                          {project.statusText}
                        </span>
                        {project.rating && (
                          <span className="flex items-center gap-1 text-sm text-yellow-600">
                            <Star className="h-4 w-4 fill-current" />
                            {project.rating}.0
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-gray-900 mb-1">{project.title}</h3>
                      {project.professional && (
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-gray-500 mb-2">
                          <User className="h-4 w-4" />
                          <span>{project.professional}</span>
                        </div>
                      )}
                      {project.budget && (
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-gray-500">
                          <DollarSign className="h-4 w-4" />
                          <span>${project.budget.toLocaleString()} MXN</span>
                          <span className="mx-1">•</span>
                          <Calendar className="h-4 w-4" />
                          <span>Inicio: {project.startDate}</span>
                        </div>
                      )}
                      {project.proposalsCount && (
                        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-purple-600">
                          <Briefcase className="h-4 w-4" />
                          <span>{project.proposalsCount} propuestas recibidas</span>
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                    
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                      {project.status === 'in_progress' && (
                        <div className="text-right">
                          <div className="text-sm text-gray-500">{project.nextMilestone}</div>
                          <div className="text-xs text-gray-400">Fecha límite: {project.nextMilestoneDate}</div>
                          <div className="w-32 bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-1.5 mt-2">
                            <div className="bg-blue-600 h-1.5 rounded-full" style={{ width: `${project.progress}%` }}></div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      )}
                      <button className="p-2 text-gray-400 hover:text-blue-600 transition">
                        <Eye className="h-5 w-5" />
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      
      case 'mensajes':
        return (
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-6">Mensajes</h2>
            <div className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-gray-100 p-6 text-center text-gray-500">
              <MessageCircle className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-3 text-gray-300" />
              <p>Próximamente: chat integrado con profesionales</p>
              <p className="text-sm">Mantente al tanto de las actualizaciones</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      
      case 'pagos':
        return (
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-6">Pagos y presupuestos</h2>
            <div className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-gray-100 p-6">
              <div className="text-center text-gray-500">
                <CreditCard className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-3 text-gray-300" />
                <p>Tus pagos están protegidos por escrow</p>
                <p className="text-sm">El dinero se libera por hitos cuando apruebas el trabajo</p>
                <button className="mt-4 text-blue-600 font-medium hover:text-blue-700">
                  Ver historial de pagos
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      
      default:
        return <div>Selecciona una opción</div>;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50">
      {/* Mobile sidebar */}
      {sidebarOpen && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 md:hidden">
          <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gray-900/50" onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)} />
          <div className="fixed inset-y-0 left-0 w-64 bg-white shadow-lg">
            <div className="flex justify-between items-center p-4 border-b">
              <span className="font-bold text-xl text-gray-900">SEMSE Project</span>
              <button onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)}>
                <X className="h-5 w-5 text-gray-500" />
              </button>
            </div>
            <nav className="p-4 space-y-2">
              {navigation.map((item) => (
                <button
                  key={item.id}
                  onClick={() => {
                    setActiveTab(item.id);
                    setSidebarOpen(false);
                  }}
                  className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg transition ${
                    activeTab === item.id
                      ? 'bg-blue-50 text-blue-600'
                      : 'text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-100'
                  }`}
                >
                  <item.icon className="h-5 w-5" />
                  <span>{item.name}</span>
                </button>
              ))}
            </nav>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Desktop Layout */}
      <div className="flex">
        {/* Sidebar desktop */}
        <aside className="hidden md:block w-64 bg-white border-r min-h-screen fixed">
          <div className="p-4 border-b">
            <span className="font-bold text-xl text-gray-900">SEMSE<span className="text-blue-600">Project</span></span>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Panel de cliente</p>
          </div>
          <nav className="p-4 space-y-2">
            {navigation.map((item) => (
              <button
                key={item.id}
                onClick={() => setActiveTab(item.id)}
                className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg transition ${
                  activeTab === item.id
                    ? 'bg-blue-50 text-blue-600'
                    : 'text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-100'
                }`}
              >
                <item.icon className="h-5 w-5" />
                <span>{item.name}</span>
              </button>
            ))}
          </nav>
          <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 right-0 p-4 border-t">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-blue-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                <User className="h-5 w-5 text-blue-600" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Juan Pérez</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">cliente@email.com</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </aside>

        {/* Main content */}
        <main className="flex-1 md:ml-64 p-4 md:p-8">
          {/* Header mobile */}
          <div className="md:hidden flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
            <button onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(true)} className="p-2">
              <Menu className="h-6 w-6 text-gray-600" />
            </button>
            <span className="font-bold text-lg">Panel de cliente</span>
            <div className="w-10" />
          </div>

          {renderContent()}
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default ClientDashboard;

                    <BarChart3 className="h-6 w-6 text-white" />
                  </div>
                  <h3 className="font-semibold text-gray-900">Reportes con IA</h3>
                </div>
                <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-4">Genera reportes automáticos de avance.</p>
                <button className="text-indigo-600 font-medium text-sm flex items-center gap-1 hover:gap-2 transition">
                  Generar reporte <ArrowRight className="h-4 w-4" />
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      
      case 'buscar':
        return (
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-6">Buscar proyectos</h2>
            <div className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-gray-100 p-6">
              <div className="flex gap-3 mb-6">
                <div className="flex-1 relative">
                  <Search className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 transform -translate-y-1/2 h-5 w-5 text-gray-400" />
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    placeholder="Buscar por tipo de proyecto, ubicación..."
                    className="w-full pl-10 pr-4 py-2 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-transparent"
                  />
                </div>
                <button className="bg-blue-600 text-white px-6 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700 transition">
                  Buscar
                </button>
              </div>
              <div className="space-y-4">
                {availableProjects.map((project) => (
                  <div key={project.id} className="border rounded-lg p-4 hover:shadow-md transition">
                    <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                      <div>
                        <h3 className="font-semibold text-gray-900">{project.title}</h3>
                        <div className="flex gap-3 text-sm text-gray-500 mt-1">
                          <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><DollarSign className="h-4 w-4" />${project.budget.toLocaleString()} MXN</span>
                          <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><MapPinIcon className="h-4 w-4" />{project.location}</span>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <button className="bg-green-600 text-white px-4 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-sm hover:bg-green-700 transition">
                        Postularme
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      
      case 'ganancias':
        return (
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-6">Mis ganancias</h2>
            <div className="bg-white rounded-xl shadow-sm border border-gray-100 p-6">
              <div className="text-center text-gray-500 py-8">
                <TrendingUp className="h-12 w-12 mx-auto mb-3 text-gray-300" />
                <p>Próximamente: panel de ganancias detallado</p>
                <p className="text-sm">Podrás ver tus ingresos, pagos pendientes y resúmenes fiscales</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      
      default:
        return <div>Selecciona una opción</div>;
    }
  };

  // Import missing icon
  const MapPinIcon = () => <MapPin className="h-4 w-4" />;

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50">
      {/* Mobile sidebar */}
      {sidebarOpen && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 md:hidden">
          <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-gray-900/50" onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)} />
          <div className="fixed inset-y-0 left-0 w-64 bg-white shadow-lg">
            <div className="flex justify-between items-center p-4 border-b">
              <span className="font-bold text-xl text-gray-900">SEMSE Project</span>
              <button onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)}>
                <X className="h-5 w-5 text-gray-500" />
              </button>
            </div>
            <nav className="p-4 space-y-2">
              {navigation.map((item) => (
                <button
                  key={item.id}
                  onClick={() => {
                    setActiveTab(item.id);
                    setSidebarOpen(false);
                  }}
                  className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg transition ${
                    activeTab === item.id
                      ? 'bg-green-50 text-green-600'
                      : 'text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-100'
                  }`}
                >
                  <item.icon className="h-5 w-5" />
                  <span>{item.name}</span>
                </button>
              ))}
            </nav>
            <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 right-0 p-4 border-t">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-green-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                  <User className="h-5 w-5 text-green-600" />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Carlos López</p>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">profesional@email.com</p>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Desktop Layout */}
      <div className="flex">
        {/* Sidebar desktop */}
        <aside className="hidden md:block w-64 bg-white border-r min-h-screen fixed">
          <div className="p-4 border-b">
            <span className="font-bold text-xl text-gray-900">SEMSE<span className="text-green-600">Project</span></span>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-1">Panel de profesional</p>
          </div>

                }`}

                <span>{item.name}</span>
              </button>
            ))}

              <div>
                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-900">Carlos López</p>
                <p className="text-xs text-gray-500">Profesional verificado</p>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </aside>

        {/* Main content */}
        <main className="flex-1 md:ml-64 p-4 md:p-8">
          {/* Header mobile */}
          <div className="md:hidden flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
            <button onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(true)} className="p-2">
              <Menu className="h-6 w-6 text-gray-600" />
            </button>
            <span className="font-bold text-lg">Panel de profesional</span>
            <div className="w-10" />
          </div>

          {renderContent()}
        </main>
      </div>
    </div>
  );

const AdminDashboard = () => {
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(false);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('overview');

  // Datos de ejemplo
  const stats = {

    totalProjects: 520,
    completedProjects: 380,

  ];

🚀 Para ejecutar la aplicación:
bash
# 1. Crear proyecto con Vite
npm create vite@latest semse-platform -- --template react
cd semse-platform

# 2. Instalar dependencias
npm install
npm install lucide-react react-router-dom

# 3. Configurar Tailwind (reemplazar los archivos)
# Copiar tailwind.config.js y src/index.css

# 4. Reemplazar src/App.jsx y crear todos los componentes

# 5. Ejecutar
npm run dev

📝 Próximos pasos recomendados:
Backend: Implementar API con NestJS/Express

Base de datos: Configurar PostgreSQL con Prisma

Autenticación: JWT + roles (cliente/profesional/admin)

Escrow: Integración con pasarela de pagos

Chat: WebSockets para mensajería en tiempo real

Prometeo IA: Integrar endpoints de análisis

Despliegue: Vercel (frontend) + Railway (backend)

¿Necesitas que implemente el backend completo con NestJS y Prisma, o que agregue alguna funcionalidad específica a los dashboards?

continua con el siguiente bloque
Perfecto. Continúo con el backend completo para SEMSE Project usando NestJS + Prisma + PostgreSQL.

🗄️ Archivo 32: backend/prisma/schema.prisma
prisma
generator client {
  provider = "prisma-client-js"
}

datasource db {
  provider = "postgresql"
  url      = env("DATABASE_URL")
}

// ==================== ENUMS ====================
enum UserRole {
  CLIENT
  PROFESSIONAL
  ADMIN
}

enum UserStatus {
  ACTIVE
  SUSPENDED
  PENDING_VERIFICATION
  BANNED
}

enum ProjectStatus {
  DRAFT
  OPEN
  IN_PROPOSAL
  IN_PROGRESS
  COMPLETED
  CANCELLED
  DISPUTED
}

enum MilestoneStatus {
  PENDING
  IN_PROGRESS
  SUBMITTED
  APPROVED
  REJECTED
  RELEASED
}

enum ProposalStatus {
  PENDING
  ACCEPTED
  REJECTED
  EXPIRED
  WITHDRAWN
}

enum EvidenceType {
  PHOTO
  VIDEO
  DOCUMENT
  CONTRACT
  INVOICE
  REPORT
}

enum EscrowStatus {
  HELD
  RELEASED
  REFUNDED
  DISPUTED
  CANCELLED
}

enum DisputeStatus {
  OPEN
  UNDER_REVIEW
  RESOLVED
  CLOSED
  ESCALATED
}

enum LeadType {
  CLIENT
  PROFESSIONAL
  COMPANY
}

enum LeadStatus {
  PENDING
  CONTACTED
  CONVERTED
  ARCHIVED
}

// ==================== MODELS ====================

model User {
  id            String    @id @default(cuid())
  email         String    @unique
  password      String
  name          String
  role          UserRole  @default(CLIENT)
  status        UserStatus @default(PENDING_VERIFICATION)
  phone         String?
  avatar        String?
  location      String?
  bio           String?
  isVerified    Boolean   @default(false)
  rating        Float     @default(0)
  reviewsCount  Int       @default(0)
  createdAt     DateTime  @default(now())
  updatedAt     DateTime  @updatedAt
  lastLogin     DateTime?
  
  // Relaciones
  clientProfile   ClientProfile?
  professionalProfile ProfessionalProfile?
  projectsAsClient   Project[]  @relation("ClientProjects")
  projectsAsProfessional Project[] @relation("ProfessionalProjects")
  proposals      Proposal[]
  evidences      Evidence[]
  messages       Message[]
  disputes       Dispute[]
  notifications  Notification[]
  
  @@map("users")
}

model ClientProfile {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId      String   @unique
  user        User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  companyName String?
  taxId       String?
  address     String?
  preferences Json?
  projects    Project[]
  
  @@map("client_profiles")
}

model ProfessionalProfile {
  id               String   @id @default(cuid())
  userId           String   @unique
  user             User     @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  oficio           String
  especialidades   String[]
  anosExperiencia  Int
  certificaciones  String[]
  areaServicio     String[]
  disponibilidad   String
  tarifaPorHora    Float?
  tarifaPorDia     Float?
  portfolio        String[]
  projects         Project[]
  
  @@map("professional_profiles")
}

model Project {
  id              String          @id @default(cuid())
  title           String
  description     String
  clientId        String
  client          User            @relation("ClientProjects", fields: [clientId], references: [id])
  professionalId  String?
  professional    User?           @relation("ProfessionalProjects", fields: [professionalId], references: [id])
  status          ProjectStatus   @default(DRAFT)
  presupuesto      Float?
  presupuestoMinimo Float?
  presupuestoMaximo Float?
  ubicacion       String
  tipoProyecto    String
  fechaInicio     DateTime?
  fechaFin        DateTime?
  duracionEstimada Int?            // días
  categories      String[]
  photos          String[]
  attachments     String[]
  milestones      Milestone[]
  proposals       Proposal[]
  evidences       Evidence[]
  contracts       Contract[]
  messages        Message[]
  disputes        Dispute[]
  prometeoAnalysis PrometeoAnalysis?
  createdAt       DateTime        @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime        @updatedAt
  
  @@map("projects")
}

model Milestone {
  id          String         @id @default(cuid())
  projectId   String
  project     Project        @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  title       String
  description String
  amount      Float
  order       Int
  status      MilestoneStatus @default(PENDING)
  evidenceId  String?
  evidence    Evidence?      @relation(fields: [evidenceId], references: [id])
  escrowId    String?
  escrow      Escrow?        @relation(fields: [escrowId], references: [id])
  dueDate     DateTime
  completedAt DateTime?
  submittedAt DateTime?
  approvedAt  DateTime?
  
  @@map("milestones")
}

model Proposal {
  id              String        @id @default(cuid())
  projectId       String
  project         Project       @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  professionalId  String
  professional    User          @relation(fields: [professionalId], references: [id])
  amount          Float
  description     String
  estimatedDays   Int
  estimatedStartDate DateTime?
  status          ProposalStatus  @default(PENDING)
  message         String?
  attachments     String[]
  createdAt       DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime      @updatedAt
  
  @@map("proposals")
}

model Evidence {
  id          String       @id @default(cuid())
  projectId   String
  project     Project      @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  milestoneId String?
  milestone   Milestone?   @relation(fields: [milestoneId], references: [id])
  userId      String
  user        User         @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id])
  type        EvidenceType
  url         String
  thumbnail   String?
  description String?
  metadata    Json?
  verifiedAt  DateTime?
  verifiedBy  String?
  createdAt   DateTime     @default(now())
  
  @@map("evidences")
}

model Contract {
  id          String    @id @default(cuid())
  projectId   String
  project     Project   @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  content     String    // URL del PDF o contenido HTML
  version     Int       @default(1)
  signedByClient Boolean @default(false)
  signedByProfessional Boolean @default(false)
  clientSignature String?
  professionalSignature String?
  signedAt    DateTime?
  expiresAt   DateTime?
  createdAt   DateTime  @default(now())
  
  @@map("contracts")
}

model Escrow {
  id            String       @id @default(cuid())
  milestoneId   String       @unique
  milestone     Milestone    @relation(fields: [milestoneId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  amount        Float
  status        EscrowStatus @default(HELD)
  paymentIntentId String?
  transactionId String?
  releaseConditions String?
  releasedAt    DateTime?
  refundedAt    DateTime?
  metadata      Json?
  createdAt     DateTime     @default(now())
  updatedAt     DateTime     @updatedAt
  
  @@map("escrow")
}

model Dispute {
  id          String        @id @default(cuid())
  projectId   String
  project     Project       @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  milestoneId String?
  raisedBy    String
  reason      String
  description String?
  status      DisputeStatus @default(OPEN)
  resolution  String?
  resolvedBy  String?
  resolvedAt  DateTime?
  evidence    String[]
  messages    Json?
  createdAt   DateTime      @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime      @updatedAt
  
  @@map("disputes")
}

model Message {
  id          String    @id @default(cuid())
  projectId   String
  project     Project   @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  senderId    String
  sender      User      @relation(fields: [senderId], references: [id])
  content     String
  attachments String[]
  isRead      Boolean   @default(false)
  readAt      DateTime?
  createdAt   DateTime  @default(now())
  
  @@map("messages")
}

model Notification {
  id          String    @id @default(cuid())
  userId      String
  user        User      @relation(fields: [userId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  title       String
  message     String
  type        String
  isRead      Boolean   @default(false)
  data        Json?
  createdAt   DateTime  @default(now())
  
  @@map("notifications")
}

model Lead {
  id          String    @id @default(cuid())
  type        LeadType
  status      LeadStatus @default(PENDING)
  data        Json      // Almacena todos los campos del formulario
  convertedTo String?   // userId si se convirtió en usuario
  notes       String?
  assignedTo  String?
  createdAt   DateTime  @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime  @updatedAt
  
  @@map("leads")
}

model PrometeoAnalysis {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  projectId   String   @unique
  project     Project  @relation(fields: [projectId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  analysis    Json     // Resultados del análisis
  recommendations Json
  riskScore   Float?
  costEstimate Float?
  durationEstimate Int?
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt
  
  @@map("prometeo_analyses")
}

model SystemLog {
  id          String   @id @default(cuid())
  level       String   // info, warn, error
  message     String
  source      String?
  metadata    Json?
  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())
  
  @@map("system_logs")
}

🚀 Archivo 34: backend/src/main.ts
typescript
import { NestFactory } from '@nestjs/core';
import { ValidationPipe } from '@nestjs/common';
import { ConfigService } from '@nestjs/config';
import { AppModule } from './app.module';

async function bootstrap() {
  const app = await NestFactory.create(AppModule);
  const configService = app.get(ConfigService);
  
  // Enable CORS
  app.enableCors({
    origin: ['http://localhost:5173', 'http://localhost:3000'],
    credentials: true,
  });
  
  // Global validation pipe
  app.useGlobalPipes(new ValidationPipe({
    whitelist: true,
    transform: true,
    forbidNonWhitelisted: true,
  }));
  
  // Global prefix
  app.setGlobalPrefix('api');
  
  const port = configService.get<number>('PORT') || 3001;
  await app.listen(port);
  console.log(`🚀 SEMSE Project Backend running on http://localhost:${port}`);
}
bootstrap();

import { Injectable, OnModuleInit, OnModuleDestroy } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaClient } from '@prisma/client';

@Injectable()
export class PrismaService extends PrismaClient implements OnModuleInit, OnModuleDestroy {
  async onModuleInit() {
    await this.$connect();
  }

  async onModuleDestroy() {
    await this.$disconnect();
  }
}
🔐 Archivo 37: backend/src/modules/auth/auth.module.ts
typescript
import { Module } from '@nestjs/common';
import { JwtModule } from '@nestjs/jwt';
import { PassportModule } from '@nestjs/passport';
import { ConfigService } from '@nestjs/config';
import { AuthService } from './auth.service';
import { AuthController } from './auth.controller';
import { JwtStrategy } from './strategies/jwt.strategy';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { UsersModule } from '../users/users.module';

@Module({
  imports: [
    PassportModule.register({ defaultStrategy: 'jwt' }),
    JwtModule.registerAsync({
      inject: [ConfigService],
      useFactory: (configService: ConfigService) => ({
        secret: configService.get('JWT_SECRET'),
        signOptions: { expiresIn: configService.get('JWT_EXPIRES_IN') || '7d' },
      }),
    }),
    UsersModule,
  ],
  controllers: [AuthController],
  providers: [AuthService, JwtStrategy, PrismaService],
  exports: [JwtStrategy, PassportModule],
})
export class AuthModule {}
🔐 Archivo 38: backend/src/modules/auth/auth.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, UnauthorizedException, ConflictException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { JwtService } from '@nestjs/jwt';
import * as bcrypt from 'bcryptjs';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { RegisterDto, LoginDto } from './dto/auth.dto';

@Injectable()
export class AuthService {
  constructor(
    private prisma: PrismaService,
    private jwtService: JwtService,
  ) {}

  async register(dto: RegisterDto) {
    // Check if user exists
    const existingUser = await this.prisma.user.findUnique({
      where: { email: dto.email },
    });
    if (existingUser) {
      throw new ConflictException('El email ya está registrado');
    }

    // Hash password
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(dto.password, 10);

    // Create user
    const user = await this.prisma.user.create({
      data: {
        email: dto.email,
        password: hashedPassword,
        name: dto.name,
        phone: dto.phone,
        role: dto.role,
        location: dto.location,
      },
    });

    // Create profile based on role
    if (dto.role === 'CLIENT' && dto.clientProfile) {
      await this.prisma.clientProfile.create({
        data: {
          userId: user.id,
          companyName: dto.clientProfile.companyName,
          taxId: dto.clientProfile.taxId,
        },
      });
    } else if (dto.role === 'PROFESSIONAL' && dto.professionalProfile) {
      await this.prisma.professionalProfile.create({
        data: {
          userId: user.id,
          oficio: dto.professionalProfile.oficio,
          especialidades: dto.professionalProfile.especialidades,
          anosExperiencia: dto.professionalProfile.anosExperiencia,
          certificaciones: dto.professionalProfile.certificaciones,
          areaServicio: dto.professionalProfile.areaServicio,
          disponibilidad: dto.professionalProfile.disponibilidad,
          tarifaPorHora: dto.professionalProfile.tarifaPorHora,
          portfolio: dto.professionalProfile.portfolio || [],
        },
      });
    }

    // Generate token
    const token = this.generateToken(user.id, user.email, user.role);

    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Usuario registrado exitosamente',
      user: {
        id: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        name: user.name,
        role: user.role,
      },
      token,
    };
  }

  async login(dto: LoginDto) {
    const user = await this.prisma.user.findUnique({
      where: { email: dto.email },
    });

    if (!user) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException('Credenciales incorrectas');
    }

    const isPasswordValid = await bcrypt.compare(dto.password, user.password);
    if (!isPasswordValid) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException('Credenciales incorrectas');
    }

    if (user.status === 'SUSPENDED' || user.status === 'BANNED') {
      throw new UnauthorizedException('Tu cuenta ha sido suspendida');
    }

    // Update last login
    await this.prisma.user.update({
      where: { id: user.id },
      data: { lastLogin: new Date() },
    });

    const token = this.generateToken(user.id, user.email, user.role);

    return {
      success: true,
      message: 'Inicio de sesión exitoso',
      user: {
        id: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        name: user.name,
        role: user.role,
        isVerified: user.isVerified,
        avatar: user.avatar,
      },
      token,
    };
  }

  private generateToken(userId: string, email: string, role: string): string {
    return this.jwtService.sign({ sub: userId, email, role });
  }

  async validateUser(userId: string) {
    return this.prisma.user.findUnique({
      where: { id: userId },
      select: {
        id: true,
        email: true,
        name: true,
        role: true,
        isVerified: true,
        status: true,
        avatar: true,
      },
    });
  }
}
🔐 Archivo 39: backend/src/modules/auth/dto/auth.dto.ts
typescript
import { IsEmail, IsString, MinLength, IsOptional, IsEnum, IsArray, IsNumber, IsObject, ValidateNested } from 'class-validator';
import { Type } from 'class-transformer';

export class ClientProfileDto {
  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  companyName?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  taxId?: string;
}

export class ProfessionalProfileDto {
  @IsString()
  oficio: string;

  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  especialidades: string[];

  @IsNumber()
  anosExperiencia: number;

  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  certificaciones: string[];

  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  areaServicio: string[];

  @IsString()
  disponibilidad: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsNumber()
  tarifaPorHora?: number;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  portfolio?: string[];
}

export class RegisterDto {
  @IsEmail()
  email: string;

  @IsString()
  @MinLength(6)
  password: string;

  @IsString()
  name: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  phone?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  location?: string;

  @IsEnum(['CLIENT', 'PROFESSIONAL', 'ADMIN'])
  role: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @ValidateNested()
  @Type(() => ClientProfileDto)
  clientProfile?: ClientProfileDto;

  @IsOptional()
  @ValidateNested()
  @Type(() => ProfessionalProfileDto)
  professionalProfile?: ProfessionalProfileDto;
}

export class LoginDto {
  @IsEmail()
  email: string;

  @IsString()
  password: string;
}

export class RefreshTokenDto {
  @IsString()
  refreshToken: string;
}
🔐 Archivo 40: backend/src/modules/auth/strategies/jwt.strategy.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, UnauthorizedException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PassportStrategy } from '@nestjs/passport';
import { ExtractJwt, Strategy } from 'passport-jwt';
import { ConfigService } from '@nestjs/config';
import { AuthService } from '../auth.service';

@Injectable()
export class JwtStrategy extends PassportStrategy(Strategy) {
  constructor(
    private configService: ConfigService,
    private authService: AuthService,
  ) {
    super({
      jwtFromRequest: ExtractJwt.fromAuthHeaderAsBearerToken(),
      ignoreExpiration: false,
      secretOrKey: configService.get('JWT_SECRET'),
    });
  }

  async validate(payload: any) {
    const user = await this.authService.validateUser(payload.sub);
    if (!user) {
      throw new UnauthorizedException();
    }
    return { ...user, ...payload };
  }
}

typescript
import { Controller, Post, Body, UseGuards, Get, Request } from '@nestjs/common';
import { AuthService } from './auth.service';
import { RegisterDto, LoginDto } from './dto/auth.dto';
import { JwtAuthGuard } from './guards/jwt-auth.guard';

@Controller('auth')
export class AuthController {
  constructor(private authService: AuthService) {}

  @Post('register')
  register(@Body() dto: RegisterDto) {
    return this.authService.register(dto);
  }

  @Post('login')
  login(@Body() dto: LoginDto) {
    return this.authService.login(dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get('me')
  getMe(@Request() req) {
    return {
      success: true,
      user: req.user,
    };
  }
}
🔐 Archivo 42: backend/src/modules/auth/guards/jwt-auth.guard.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, ExecutionContext, UnauthorizedException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { AuthGuard } from '@nestjs/passport';

@Injectable()
export class JwtAuthGuard extends AuthGuard('jwt') {
  canActivate(context: ExecutionContext) {
    return super.canActivate(context);
  }

  handleRequest(err, user, info) {
    if (err || !user) {
      throw err || new UnauthorizedException('No autorizado');
    }
    return user;
  }
}

👤 Archivo 44: backend/src/modules/users/users.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, NotFoundException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { UpdateUserDto, UpdateProfessionalProfileDto } from './dto/user.dto';

@Injectable()
export class UsersService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async findById(id: string) {
    const user = await this.prisma.user.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: {
        clientProfile: true,
        professionalProfile: true,
      },
    });
    if (!user) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Usuario no encontrado');
    }
    return user;
  }

  async updateUser(id: string, dto: UpdateUserDto) {
    return this.prisma.user.update({
      where: { id },
      data: {
        name: dto.name,
        phone: dto.phone,
        location: dto.location,
        bio: dto.bio,
        avatar: dto.avatar,
      },
      select: {
        id: true,
        email: true,
        name: true,
        role: true,
        phone: true,
        location: true,
        bio: true,
        avatar: true,
        isVerified: true,
        rating: true,
      },
    });
  }

  async updateProfessionalProfile(userId: string, dto: UpdateProfessionalProfileDto) {
    const professional = await this.prisma.professionalProfile.findUnique({
      where: { userId },
    });
    if (!professional) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Perfil profesional no encontrado');
    }

    return this.prisma.professionalProfile.update({
      where: { userId },
      data: {
        oficio: dto.oficio,
        especialidades: dto.especialidades,
        anosExperiencia: dto.anosExperiencia,
        certificaciones: dto.certificaciones,
        areaServicio: dto.areaServicio,
        disponibilidad: dto.disponibilidad,
        tarifaPorHora: dto.tarifaPorHora,
        tarifaPorDia: dto.tarifaPorDia,
        portfolio: dto.portfolio,
      },
    });
  }

  async getDashboardData(userId: string, role: string) {
    if (role === 'CLIENT') {
      const projects = await this.prisma.project.findMany({
        where: { clientId: userId },
        include: {
          professional: {
            select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true },
          },
          milestones: true,
        },
        orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
      });

      const stats = {
        totalProjects: projects.length,
        completedProjects: projects.filter(p => p.status === 'COMPLETED').length,
        inProgressProjects: projects.filter(p => p.status === 'IN_PROGRESS').length,
        totalSpent: projects.reduce((sum, p) => sum + (p.presupuesto || 0), 0),
      };

      return { projects, stats };
    } else if (role === 'PROFESSIONAL') {
      const projects = await this.prisma.project.findMany({
        where: { professionalId: userId },
        include: {
          client: {
            select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true },
          },
          milestones: true,
        },
        orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
      });

      const availableProjects = await this.prisma.project.findMany({
        where: { status: 'OPEN', professionalId: null },
        take: 10,
        orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
      });

      const stats = {
        totalProjects: projects.length,
        completedProjects: projects.filter(p => p.status === 'COMPLETED').length,
        inProgressProjects: projects.filter(p => p.status === 'IN_PROGRESS').length,
        totalEarned: projects
          .filter(p => p.status === 'COMPLETED')
          .reduce((sum, p) => sum + (p.presupuesto || 0), 0),
      };

      return { projects, availableProjects, stats };
    }

    return null;
  }
}
👤 Archivo 45: backend/src/modules/users/users.controller.ts
typescript
import { Controller, Get, Put, Body, UseGuards, Request, Param } from '@nestjs/common';
import { UsersService } from './users.service';
import { JwtAuthGuard } from '../auth/guards/jwt-auth.guard';
import { UpdateUserDto, UpdateProfessionalProfileDto } from './dto/user.dto';

@Controller('users')
export class UsersController {
  constructor(private usersService: UsersService) {}

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get('me')
  getProfile(@Request() req) {
    return this.usersService.findById(req.user.id);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Put('me')
  updateProfile(@Request() req, @Body() dto: UpdateUserDto) {
    return this.usersService.updateUser(req.user.id, dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Put('me/professional')
  updateProfessionalProfile(@Request() req, @Body() dto: UpdateProfessionalProfileDto) {
    return this.usersService.updateProfessionalProfile(req.user.id, dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get('dashboard')
  getDashboard(@Request() req) {
    return this.usersService.getDashboardData(req.user.id, req.user.role);
  }

  @Get(':id')
  getUser(@Param('id') id: string) {
    return this.usersService.findById(id);
  }
}

import { IsOptional, IsString, IsEmail, IsNumber, IsArray, MinLength } from 'class-validator';

export class UpdateUserDto {
  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  name?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  phone?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  location?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  bio?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  avatar?: string;
}

export class UpdateProfessionalProfileDto {
  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  oficio?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  especialidades?: string[];

  @IsOptional()
  @IsNumber()
  anosExperiencia?: number;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  certificaciones?: string[];

  @IsOptional()
  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  areaServicio?: string[];

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  disponibilidad?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsNumber()
  tarifaPorHora?: number;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsNumber()
  tarifaPorDia?: number;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  portfolio?: string[];
}

📋 Archivo 48: backend/src/modules/leads/leads.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { CreateClientLeadDto, CreateProfessionalLeadDto, CreateCompanyLeadDto } from './dto/lead.dto';

@Injectable()
export class LeadsService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async createClientLead(dto: CreateClientLeadDto) {
    return this.prisma.lead.create({
      data: {
        type: 'CLIENT',
        data: dto as any,
        status: 'PENDING',
      },
    });
  }

  async createProfessionalLead(dto: CreateProfessionalLeadDto) {
    return this.prisma.lead.create({
      data: {
        type: 'PROFESSIONAL',
        data: dto as any,
        status: 'PENDING',
      },
    });
  }

  async createCompanyLead(dto: CreateCompanyLeadDto) {
    return this.prisma.lead.create({
      data: {
        type: 'COMPANY',
        data: dto as any,
        status: 'PENDING',
      },
    });
  }

  async findAll() {
    return this.prisma.lead.findMany({
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async findOne(id: string) {
    return this.prisma.lead.findUnique({
      where: { id },
    });
  }

  async updateStatus(id: string, status: string, convertedTo?: string) {
    return this.prisma.lead.update({
      where: { id },
      data: { status, convertedTo },
    });
  }
}

📋 Archivo 50: backend/src/modules/leads/leads.controller.ts
typescript
import { Controller, Post, Body, Get, Param, UseGuards } from '@nestjs/common';
import { LeadsService } from './leads.service';
import { CreateClientLeadDto, CreateProfessionalLeadDto, CreateCompanyLeadDto } from './dto/lead.dto';
import { JwtAuthGuard } from '../auth/guards/jwt-auth.guard';

@Controller('leads')
export class LeadsController {
  constructor(private leadsService: LeadsService) {}

  @Post('client')
  createClientLead(@Body() dto: CreateClientLeadDto) {
    return this.leadsService.createClientLead(dto);
  }

  @Post('professional')
  createProfessionalLead(@Body() dto: CreateProfessionalLeadDto) {
    return this.leadsService.createProfessionalLead(dto);
  }

  @Post('company')
  createCompanyLead(@Body() dto: CreateCompanyLeadDto) {
    return this.leadsService.createCompanyLead(dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get()
  findAll() {
    return this.leadsService.findAll();
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get(':id')
  findOne(@Param('id') id: string) {
    return this.leadsService.findOne(id);
  }
}

📁 Archivo 53: backend/src/modules/projects/projects.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, NotFoundException, ForbiddenException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { CreateProjectDto, UpdateProjectDto, AddMilestoneDto } from './dto/project.dto';

@Injectable()
export class ProjectsService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async create(clientId: string, dto: CreateProjectDto) {
    return this.prisma.project.create({
      data: {
        title: dto.title,
        description: dto.description,
        clientId: clientId,
        presupuesto: dto.presupuesto,
        presupuestoMinimo: dto.presupuestoMinimo,
        presupuestoMaximo: dto.presupuestoMaximo,
        ubicacion: dto.ubicacion,
        tipoProyecto: dto.tipoProyecto,
        categories: dto.categories,
        duracionEstimada: dto.duracionEstimada,
        status: 'OPEN',
      },
      include: {
        client: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, email: true, avatar: true },
        },
      },
    });
  }

  async findAll(filters?: {
    status?: string;
    tipoProyecto?: string;
    ubicacion?: string;
    minPresupuesto?: number;
    maxPresupuesto?: number;
  }) {
    const where: any = {};
    
    if (filters?.status) where.status = filters.status;
    if (filters?.tipoProyecto) where.tipoProyecto = filters.tipoProyecto;
    if (filters?.ubicacion) where.ubicacion = { contains: filters.ubicacion, mode: 'insensitive' };
    if (filters?.minPresupuesto) where.presupuesto = { gte: filters.minPresupuesto };
    if (filters?.maxPresupuesto) where.presupuesto = { ...where.presupuesto, lte: filters.maxPresupuesto };

    return this.prisma.project.findMany({
      where,
      include: {
        client: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true },
        },
        professional: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true },
        },
        proposals: {
          where: { status: 'PENDING' },
          select: { id: true, amount: true, professional: { select: { id: true, name: true, rating: true } } },
        },
        milestones: true,
        _count: {
          select: { proposals: true, milestones: true },
        },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async findOne(id: string) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: {
        client: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, email: true, phone: true, avatar: true, rating: true },
        },
        professional: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, email: true, phone: true, avatar: true, rating: true },
        },
        proposals: {
          include: {
            professional: {
              select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true, professionalProfile: true },
            },
          },
          orderBy: { amount: 'asc' },
        },
        milestones: {
          orderBy: { order: 'asc' },
          include: { evidence: true, escrow: true },
        },
        evidences: {
          orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
          take: 10,
        },
        messages: {
          orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
          take: 50,
          include: { sender: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, role: true } } },
        },
        contracts: true,
        prometeoAnalysis: true,
      },
    });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    return project;
  }

  async update(id: string, userId: string, userRole: string, dto: UpdateProjectDto) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({ where: { id } });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    if (project.clientId !== userId && userRole !== 'ADMIN') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('No tienes permiso para editar este proyecto');
    }

    return this.prisma.project.update({
      where: { id },
      data: {
        title: dto.title,
        description: dto.description,
        presupuesto: dto.presupuesto,
        presupuestoMinimo: dto.presupuestoMinimo,
        presupuestoMaximo: dto.presupuestoMaximo,
        ubicacion: dto.ubicacion,
        tipoProyecto: dto.tipoProyecto,
        categories: dto.categories,
        duracionEstimada: dto.duracionEstimada,
        status: dto.status,
      },
      include: {
        client: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true } },
        professional: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true } },
      },
    });
  }

  async delete(id: string, userId: string, userRole: string) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({ where: { id } });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    if (project.clientId !== userId && userRole !== 'ADMIN') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('No tienes permiso para eliminar este proyecto');
    }

    return this.prisma.project.delete({ where: { id } });
  }

  async assignProfessional(projectId: string, professionalId: string, proposalId: string) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({ where: { id: projectId } });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    // Actualizar proyecto
    const updatedProject = await this.prisma.project.update({
      where: { id: projectId },
      data: {
        professionalId: professionalId,
        status: 'IN_PROGRESS',
      },
    });

    // Actualizar propuesta a ACCEPTED
    await this.prisma.proposal.update({
      where: { id: proposalId },
      data: { status: 'ACCEPTED' },
    });

    // Rechazar otras propuestas
    await this.prisma.proposal.updateMany({
      where: { projectId, id: { not: proposalId } },
      data: { status: 'REJECTED' },
    });

    return updatedProject;
  }

  async addMilestone(projectId: string, userId: string, dto: AddMilestoneDto) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({ where: { id: projectId } });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    if (project.clientId !== userId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Solo el cliente puede agregar hitos');
    }

    const milestoneCount = await this.prisma.milestone.count({
      where: { projectId },
    });

    return this.prisma.milestone.create({
      data: {
        projectId,
        title: dto.title,
        description: dto.description,
        amount: dto.amount,
        order: milestoneCount,
        dueDate: dto.dueDate,
      },
    });
  }

  async getClientProjects(clientId: string) {
    return this.prisma.project.findMany({
      where: { clientId },
      include: {
        professional: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true } },
        milestones: true,
        _count: { select: { proposals: true } },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async getProfessionalProjects(professionalId: string) {
    return this.prisma.project.findMany({
      where: { professionalId },
      include: {
        client: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true } },
        milestones: true,
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async getAvailableProjects(professionalId: string) {
    const professional = await this.prisma.professionalProfile.findUnique({
      where: { userId: professionalId },
    });

    if (!professional) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Perfil profesional no encontrado');
    }

    return this.prisma.project.findMany({
      where: {
        status: 'OPEN',
        professionalId: null,
        tipoProyecto: { in: professional.especialidades },
      },
      include: {
        client: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true } },
        _count: { select: { proposals: true } },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
      take: 20,
    });
  }

  async updateStatus(id: string, status: string, userId: string, userRole: string) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({ where: { id } });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    if (project.clientId !== userId && project.professionalId !== userId && userRole !== 'ADMIN') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('No tienes permiso para actualizar este proyecto');
    }

    return this.prisma.project.update({
      where: { id },
      data: { status },
    });
  }
}

import { Controller, Get, Post, Put, Delete, Body, Param, Query, UseGuards, Request } from '@nestjs/common';
import { ProjectsService } from './projects.service';
import { CreateProjectDto, UpdateProjectDto, AddMilestoneDto } from './dto/project.dto';
import { JwtAuthGuard } from '../auth/guards/jwt-auth.guard';

@Controller('projects')
export class ProjectsController {
  constructor(private projectsService: ProjectsService) {}

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post()
  create(@Request() req, @Body() dto: CreateProjectDto) {
    return this.projectsService.create(req.user.id, dto);
  }

  @Get()
  findAll(@Query() query: any) {
    return this.projectsService.findAll(query);
  }

  @Get('available')
  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  getAvailable(@Request() req) {
    return this.projectsService.getAvailableProjects(req.user.id);
  }

  @Get('my-projects')
  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  getMyProjects(@Request() req) {
    if (req.user.role === 'CLIENT') {
      return this.projectsService.getClientProjects(req.user.id);
    } else if (req.user.role === 'PROFESSIONAL') {
      return this.projectsService.getProfessionalProjects(req.user.id);
    }
    return [];
  }

  @Get(':id')
  findOne(@Param('id') id: string) {
    return this.projectsService.findOne(id);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Put(':id')
  update(@Param('id') id: string, @Request() req, @Body() dto: UpdateProjectDto) {
    return this.projectsService.update(id, req.user.id, req.user.role, dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Delete(':id')
  remove(@Param('id') id: string, @Request() req) {
    return this.projectsService.delete(id, req.user.id, req.user.role);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post(':id/assign/:professionalId/:proposalId')
  assignProfessional(
    @Param('id') id: string,
    @Param('professionalId') professionalId: string,
    @Param('proposalId') proposalId: string,
  ) {
    return this.projectsService.assignProfessional(id, professionalId, proposalId);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post(':id/milestones')
  addMilestone(@Param('id') id: string, @Request() req, @Body() dto: AddMilestoneDto) {
    return this.projectsService.addMilestone(id, req.user.id, dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Put(':id/status')
  updateStatus(@Param('id') id: string, @Body('status') status: string, @Request() req) {
    return this.projectsService.updateStatus(id, status, req.user.id, req.user.role);
  }
}

📁 Archivo 57: backend/src/modules/proposals/proposals.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, NotFoundException, ForbiddenException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { CreateProposalDto } from './dto/proposal.dto';

@Injectable()
export class ProposalsService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async create(professionalId: string, projectId: string, dto: CreateProposalDto) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({
      where: { id: projectId },
    });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    const existingProposal = await this.prisma.proposal.findFirst({
      where: { projectId, professionalId, status: 'PENDING' },
    });

    if (existingProposal) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Ya tienes una propuesta pendiente para este proyecto');
    }

    return this.prisma.proposal.create({
      data: {
        projectId,
        professionalId,
        amount: dto.amount,
        description: dto.description,
        estimatedDays: dto.estimatedDays,
        estimatedStartDate: dto.estimatedStartDate,
        message: dto.message,
        attachments: dto.attachments || [],
      },
      include: {
        professional: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true },
        },
      },
    });
  }

  async findByProject(projectId: string) {
    return this.prisma.proposal.findMany({
      where: { projectId },
      include: {
        professional: {
          select: {
            id: true,
            name: true,
            avatar: true,
            rating: true,
            professionalProfile: true,
          },
        },
      },
      orderBy: { amount: 'asc' },
    });
  }

  async findByProfessional(professionalId: string) {
    return this.prisma.proposal.findMany({
      where: { professionalId },
      include: {
        project: {
          select: { id: true, title: true, description: true, ubicacion: true, client: true },
        },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async updateStatus(id: string, professionalId: string, status: string) {
    const proposal = await this.prisma.proposal.findUnique({
      where: { id },
    });

    if (!proposal) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Propuesta no encontrada');
    }

    if (proposal.professionalId !== professionalId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('No tienes permiso para modificar esta propuesta');
    }

    return this.prisma.proposal.update({
      where: { id },
      data: { status },
    });
  }

  async withdraw(proposalId: string, professionalId: string) {
    const proposal = await this.prisma.proposal.findUnique({
      where: { id: proposalId },
    });

    if (!proposal) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Propuesta no encontrada');
    }

    if (proposal.professionalId !== professionalId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('No tienes permiso para retirar esta propuesta');
    }

    return this.prisma.proposal.update({
      where: { id: proposalId },
      data: { status: 'WITHDRAWN' },
    });
  }

  async getProposalById(id: string) {
    const proposal = await this.prisma.proposal.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: {
        project: {
          include: {
            client: { select: { id: true, name: true, email: true, phone: true } },
          },
        },
        professional: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, rating: true, professionalProfile: true },
        },
      },
    });

    if (!proposal) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Propuesta no encontrada');
    }

    return proposal;
  }
}

📁 Archivo 61: backend/src/modules/milestones/milestones.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, NotFoundException, ForbiddenException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { SubmitMilestoneDto, ApproveMilestoneDto } from './dto/milestone.dto';

@Injectable()
export class MilestonesService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async findByProject(projectId: string) {
    return this.prisma.milestone.findMany({
      where: { projectId },
      include: {
        evidence: true,
        escrow: true,
      },
      orderBy: { order: 'asc' },
    });
  }

  async findOne(id: string) {
    const milestone = await this.prisma.milestone.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: {
        project: {
          select: { id: true, title: true, clientId: true, professionalId: true },
        },
        evidence: true,
        escrow: true,
      },
    });

    if (!milestone) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Hito no encontrado');
    }

    return milestone;
  }

  async submitMilestone(milestoneId: string, professionalId: string, dto: SubmitMilestoneDto) {
    const milestone = await this.prisma.milestone.findUnique({
      where: { id: milestoneId },
      include: { project: true },
    });

    if (!milestone) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Hito no encontrado');
    }

    if (milestone.project.professionalId !== professionalId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Solo el profesional asignado puede entregar hitos');
    }

    if (milestone.status !== 'IN_PROGRESS' && milestone.status !== 'PENDING') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Este hito no puede ser entregado en este momento');
    }

    let evidenceId = null;
    if (dto.evidenceUrl) {
      const evidence = await this.prisma.evidence.create({
        data: {
          projectId: milestone.projectId,
          milestoneId: milestone.id,
          userId: professionalId,
          type: dto.evidenceType || 'PHOTO',
          url: dto.evidenceUrl,
          description: dto.evidenceDescription,
        },
      });
      evidenceId = evidence.id;
    }

    return this.prisma.milestone.update({
      where: { id: milestoneId },
      data: {
        status: 'SUBMITTED',
        evidenceId: evidenceId,
        submittedAt: new Date(),
      },
    });
  }

  async approveMilestone(milestoneId: string, clientId: string, dto: ApproveMilestoneDto) {
    const milestone = await this.prisma.milestone.findUnique({
      where: { id: milestoneId },
      include: { project: true },
    });

    if (!milestone) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Hito no encontrado');
    }

    if (milestone.project.clientId !== clientId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Solo el cliente puede aprobar hitos');
    }

    if (milestone.status !== 'SUBMITTED') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Este hito no está pendiente de aprobación');
    }

    const updatedMilestone = await this.prisma.milestone.update({
      where: { id: milestoneId },
      data: {
        status: dto.approved ? 'APPROVED' : 'REJECTED',
        approvedAt: dto.approved ? new Date() : null,
      },
    });

    // Si es aprobado, crear solicitud de liberación de pago al escrow
    if (dto.approved && milestone.escrowId) {
      // Aquí se integraría con el módulo de escrow
      // await this.escrowService.requestRelease(milestone.escrowId);
    }

    return updatedMilestone;
  }

  async startMilestone(milestoneId: string, professionalId: string) {
    const milestone = await this.prisma.milestone.findUnique({
      where: { id: milestoneId },
      include: { project: true },
    });

    if (!milestone) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Hito no encontrado');
    }

    if (milestone.project.professionalId !== professionalId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Solo el profesional asignado puede iniciar hitos');
    }

    if (milestone.status !== 'PENDING') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Este hito ya ha sido iniciado');
    }

    return this.prisma.milestone.update({
      where: { id: milestoneId },
      data: { status: 'IN_PROGRESS' },
    });
  }

  async getMilestoneProgress(projectId: string) {
    const milestones = await this.prisma.milestone.findMany({
      where: { projectId },
    });

    const total = milestones.length;
    const completed = milestones.filter(m => m.status === 'APPROVED' || m.status === 'RELEASED').length;
    const inProgress = milestones.filter(m => m.status === 'IN_PROGRESS' || m.status === 'SUBMITTED').length;

    return {
      total,
      completed,
      inProgress,
      percentage: total > 0 ? (completed / total) * 100 : 0,
    };
  }
}

📁 Archivo 65: backend/src/modules/evidence/evidence.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, NotFoundException, ForbiddenException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { CreateEvidenceDto, VerifyEvidenceDto } from './dto/evidence.dto';

@Injectable()
export class EvidenceService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async create(userId: string, projectId: string, dto: CreateEvidenceDto) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({
      where: { id: projectId },
    });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    if (project.clientId !== userId && project.professionalId !== userId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('No tienes permiso para agregar evidencias');
    }

    return this.prisma.evidence.create({
      data: {
        projectId,
        userId,
        milestoneId: dto.milestoneId,
        type: dto.type,
        url: dto.url,
        description: dto.description,
        metadata: dto.metadata,
      },
    });
  }

  async findByProject(projectId: string) {
    return this.prisma.evidence.findMany({
      where: { projectId },
      include: {
        user: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, role: true } },
        milestone: { select: { id: true, title: true } },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async findByMilestone(milestoneId: string) {
    return this.prisma.evidence.findMany({
      where: { milestoneId },
      include: {
        user: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true } },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async verify(id: string, adminId: string, dto: VerifyEvidenceDto) {
    const evidence = await this.prisma.evidence.findUnique({
      where: { id },
    });

    if (!evidence) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Evidencia no encontrada');
    }

    return this.prisma.evidence.update({
      where: { id },
      data: {
        verifiedAt: new Date(),
        verifiedBy: adminId,
      },
    });
  }

  async delete(id: string, userId: string, userRole: string) {
    const evidence = await this.prisma.evidence.findUnique({
      where: { id },
    });

    if (!evidence) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Evidencia no encontrada');
    }

    if (evidence.userId !== userId && userRole !== 'ADMIN') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('No tienes permiso para eliminar esta evidencia');
    }

    return this.prisma.evidence.delete({ where: { id } });
  }

  async getVerificationStatus(projectId: string) {
    const evidences = await this.prisma.evidence.findMany({
      where: { projectId },
    });

    const total = evidences.length;
    const verified = evidences.filter(e => e.verifiedAt !== null).length;

    return {
      total,
      verified,
      pending: total - verified,
      percentage: total > 0 ? (verified / total) * 100 : 0,
    };
  }
}

📁 Archivo 67: backend/src/modules/evidence/dto/evidence.dto.ts

import { IsString, IsOptional, IsEnum, IsObject } from 'class-validator';

export class CreateEvidenceDto {
  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  milestoneId?: string;

  @IsEnum(['PHOTO', 'VIDEO', 'DOCUMENT', 'CONTRACT', 'INVOICE', 'REPORT'])
  type: string;

  @IsString()
  url: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  description?: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsObject()
  metadata?: Record<string, any>;
}

export class VerifyEvidenceDto {
  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  notes?: string;
}

📁 Archivo 69: backend/src/modules/escrow/escrow.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, NotFoundException, ForbiddenException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { CreateEscrowDto, ReleaseEscrowDto } from './dto/escrow.dto';

@Injectable()
export class EscrowService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async create(milestoneId: string, dto: CreateEscrowDto) {
    const milestone = await this.prisma.milestone.findUnique({
      where: { id: milestoneId },
      include: { project: true },
    });

    if (!milestone) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Hito no encontrado');
    }

    const existingEscrow = await this.prisma.escrow.findUnique({
      where: { milestoneId },
    });

    if (existingEscrow) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Este hito ya tiene un escrow asociado');
    }

    return this.prisma.escrow.create({
      data: {
        milestoneId,
        amount: dto.amount || milestone.amount,
        paymentIntentId: dto.paymentIntentId,
        metadata: dto.metadata,
      },
      include: {
        milestone: {
          include: { project: { select: { id: true, title: true } } },
        },
      },
    });
  }

  async findByMilestone(milestoneId: string) {
    return this.prisma.escrow.findUnique({
      where: { milestoneId },
      include: {
        milestone: {
          include: { project: { select: { id: true, title: true, clientId: true, professionalId: true } } },
        },
      },
    });
  }

  async findByProject(projectId: string) {
    return this.prisma.escrow.findMany({
      where: { milestone: { projectId } },
      include: {
        milestone: { select: { id: true, title: true, order: true } },
      },
    });
  }

  async requestRelease(milestoneId: string, userId: string) {
    const escrow = await this.prisma.escrow.findUnique({
      where: { milestoneId },
      include: { milestone: { include: { project: true } } },
    });

    if (!escrow) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Escrow no encontrado');
    }

    if (escrow.status !== 'HELD') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('El escrow no está en estado HELD');
    }

    if (escrow.milestone.project.professionalId !== userId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('Solo el profesional puede solicitar liberación');
    }

    if (escrow.milestone.status !== 'APPROVED') {
      throw new ForbiddenException('El hito debe estar aprobado para solicitar liberación');
    }

    return this.prisma.escrow.update({
      where: { milestoneId },
      data: { status: 'RELEASED', releasedAt: new Date() },
    });
  }

  async release(milestoneId: string, adminId: string, dto: ReleaseEscrowDto) {
    const escrow = await this.prisma.escrow.findUnique({
      where: { milestoneId },
      include: { milestone: true },
    });

    if (!escrow) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Escrow no encontrado');
    }

    // Aquí se integraría con Stripe para liberar el pago
    // await this.stripeService.releasePayment(escrow.paymentIntentId);

    return this.prisma.escrow.update({
      where: { milestoneId },
      data: {
        status: 'RELEASED',
        releasedAt: new Date(),
        releaseConditions: dto.notes,
      },
    });
  }

  async refund(milestoneId: string, adminId: string, reason: string) {
    const escrow = await this.prisma.escrow.findUnique({
      where: { milestoneId },
    });

    if (!escrow) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Escrow no encontrado');
    }

    // Aquí se integraría con Stripe para reembolsar
    // await this.stripeService.refundPayment(escrow.paymentIntentId);

    return this.prisma.escrow.update({
      where: { milestoneId },
      data: {
        status: 'REFUNDED',
        refundedAt: new Date(),
      },
    });
  }

  async getTotalHeld(clientId: string) {
    const escrows = await this.prisma.escrow.findMany({
      where: {
        milestone: {
          project: { clientId },
          status: { in: ['APPROVED', 'SUBMITTED'] },
        },
        status: 'HELD',
      },
    });

    return escrows.reduce((sum, e) => sum + e.amount, 0);
  }

  async getTotalEarned(professionalId: string) {
    const escrows = await this.prisma.escrow.findMany({
      where: {
        milestone: {
          project: { professionalId },
        },
        status: 'RELEASED',
      },
    });

    return escrows.reduce((sum, e) => sum + e.amount, 0);
  }
}

@Controller('escrow')
export class EscrowController {

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)

  @Get('professional/total-earned')
