📁 Archivo 73: backend/src/modules/chat/chat.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { SendMessageDto } from './dto/chat.dto';

@Injectable()
export class ChatService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async sendMessage(senderId: string, projectId: string, dto: SendMessageDto) {
    const message = await this.prisma.message.create({
      data: {
        projectId,
        senderId,
        content: dto.content,
        attachments: dto.attachments || [],
      },
      include: {
        sender: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, role: true },
        },
      },
    });

    // Marcar como no leído para el otro participante
    await this.prisma.$executeRaw`
      UPDATE messages SET is_read = false 
      WHERE project_id = ${projectId} AND sender_id != ${senderId}
    `;

    return message;
  }

  async getMessages(projectId: string, limit: number = 50, beforeDate?: Date) {
    const where: any = { projectId };
    if (beforeDate) {
      where.createdAt = { lt: beforeDate };
    }

    return this.prisma.message.findMany({
      where,
      include: {
        sender: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true, role: true },
        },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
      take: limit,
    });
  }

  async markAsRead(messageId: string, userId: string) {
    const message = await this.prisma.message.findUnique({
      where: { id: messageId },
    });

    if (message && message.senderId !== userId) {
      await this.prisma.message.update({
        where: { id: messageId },
        data: { isRead: true, readAt: new Date() },
      });
    }

    return { success: true };
  }

  async markProjectAsRead(projectId: string, userId: string) {
    await this.prisma.message.updateMany({
      where: {
        projectId,
        senderId: { not: userId },
        isRead: false,
      },
      data: { isRead: true, readAt: new Date() },
    });

    return { success: true };
  }

  async getUnreadCount(userId: string) {
    const count = await this.prisma.message.count({
      where: {
        senderId: { not: userId },
        isRead: false,
        project: {
          OR: [
            { clientId: userId },
            { professionalId: userId },
          ],
        },
      },
    });

    return { count };
  }

  async getConversations(userId: string) {
    const messages = await this.prisma.message.groupBy({
      by: ['projectId'],
      where: {
        project: {
          OR: [
            { clientId: userId },
            { professionalId: userId },
          ],
        },
      },
      orderBy: {
        _max: { createdAt: 'desc' },
      },
    });

    const conversations = await Promise.all(
      messages.map(async (msg) => {
        const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({
          where: { id: msg.projectId },
          select: {
            id: true,
            title: true,
            client: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true } },
            professional: { select: { id: true, name: true, avatar: true } },
          },
        });

        const lastMessage = await this.prisma.message.findFirst({
          where: { projectId: msg.projectId },
          orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
        });

        const unreadCount = await this.prisma.message.count({
          where: {
            projectId: msg.projectId,
            senderId: { not: userId },
            isRead: false,
          },
        });

        return {
          project,
          lastMessage,
          unreadCount,
        };
      })
    );

    return conversations;
  }
}

import { Controller, Get, Post, Body, Param, Query, UseGuards, Request } from '@nestjs/common';
import { ChatService } from './chat.service';
import { SendMessageDto } from './dto/chat.dto';
import { JwtAuthGuard } from '../auth/guards/jwt-auth.guard';

@Controller('chat')
export class ChatController {
  constructor(private chatService: ChatService) {}

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post('project/:projectId')
  sendMessage(@Request() req, @Param('projectId') projectId: string, @Body() dto: SendMessageDto) {
    return this.chatService.sendMessage(req.user.id, projectId, dto);
  }

  @Get('project/:projectId')
  getMessages(@Param('projectId') projectId: string, @Query('limit') limit?: string, @Query('before') before?: string) {
    return this.chatService.getMessages(projectId, limit ? parseInt(limit) : 50, before ? new Date(before) : undefined);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post('message/:messageId/read')
  markAsRead(@Param('messageId') messageId: string, @Request() req) {
    return this.chatService.markAsRead(messageId, req.user.id);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post('project/:projectId/read')
  markProjectAsRead(@Param('projectId') projectId: string, @Request() req) {
    return this.chatService.markProjectAsRead(projectId, req.user.id);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get('unread/count')
  getUnreadCount(@Request() req) {
    return this.chatService.getUnreadCount(req.user.id);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get('conversations')
  getConversations(@Request() req) {
    return this.chatService.getConversations(req.user.id);
  }
}

📁 Archivo 77: backend/src/modules/disputes/disputes.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable, NotFoundException, ForbiddenException } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { CreateDisputeDto, ResolveDisputeDto } from './dto/dispute.dto';

@Injectable()
export class DisputesService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async create(userId: string, dto: CreateDisputeDto) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({
      where: { id: dto.projectId },
    });

    if (!project) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Proyecto no encontrado');
    }

    if (project.clientId !== userId && project.professionalId !== userId) {
      throw new ForbiddenException('No tienes permiso para crear disputas en este proyecto');
    }

    // Actualizar estado del proyecto a DISPUTED
    await this.prisma.project.update({
      where: { id: dto.projectId },
      data: { status: 'DISPUTED' },
    });

    if (dto.milestoneId) {
      await this.prisma.milestone.update({
        where: { id: dto.milestoneId },
        data: { status: 'PENDING' },
      });
    }

    return this.prisma.dispute.create({
      data: {
        projectId: dto.projectId,
        milestoneId: dto.milestoneId,
        raisedBy: userId,
        reason: dto.reason,
        description: dto.description,
        evidence: dto.evidence || [],
      },
      include: {
        project: { select: { id: true, title: true } },
      },
    });
  }

  async findAll() {
    return this.prisma.dispute.findMany({
      include: {
        project: { select: { id: true, title: true, client: true, professional: true } },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async findOne(id: string) {
    const dispute = await this.prisma.dispute.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: {
        project: {
          include: {
            client: { select: { id: true, name: true, email: true, phone: true } },
            professional: { select: { id: true, name: true, email: true, phone: true } },
          },
        },
      },
    });

    if (!dispute) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Disputa no encontrada');
    }

    return dispute;
  }

  async findByProject(projectId: string) {
    return this.prisma.dispute.findMany({
      where: { projectId },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async findByUser(userId: string) {
    return this.prisma.dispute.findMany({
      where: {
        OR: [
          { raisedBy: userId },
          { project: { clientId: userId } },
          { project: { professionalId: userId } },
        ],
      },
      include: {
        project: { select: { id: true, title: true } },
      },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });
  }

  async updateStatus(id: string, adminId: string, status: string) {
    const dispute = await this.prisma.dispute.findUnique({
      where: { id },
    });

    if (!dispute) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Disputa no encontrada');
    }

    return this.prisma.dispute.update({
      where: { id },
      data: { status },
    });
  }

  async resolve(id: string, adminId: string, dto: ResolveDisputeDto) {
    const dispute = await this.prisma.dispute.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: { project: true },
    });

    if (!dispute) {
      throw new NotFoundException('Disputa no encontrada');
    }

    // Actualizar estado del proyecto
    await this.prisma.project.update({
      where: { id: dispute.projectId },
      data: { status: dto.projectNewStatus || 'IN_PROGRESS' },
    });

    return this.prisma.dispute.update({
      where: { id },
      data: {
        status: 'RESOLVED',
        resolution: dto.resolution,
        resolvedBy: adminId,
        resolvedAt: new Date(),
      },
    });
  }

  async getStatistics() {
    const stats = await this.prisma.dispute.groupBy({
      by: ['status'],
      _count: true,
    });

    const openCount = stats.find(s => s.status === 'OPEN')?._count || 0;
    const underReviewCount = stats.find(s => s.status === 'UNDER_REVIEW')?._count || 0;
    const resolvedCount = stats.find(s => s.status === 'RESOLVED')?._count || 0;

    return {
      open: openCount,
      underReview: underReviewCount,
      resolved: resolvedCount,
      total: openCount + underReviewCount + resolvedCount,
    };
  }
}
📁 Archivo 78: backend/src/modules/disputes/disputes.controller.ts

import { Controller, Get, Post, Put, Body, Param, UseGuards, Request } from '@nestjs/common';
import { DisputesService } from './disputes.service';
import { CreateDisputeDto, ResolveDisputeDto } from './dto/dispute.dto';
import { JwtAuthGuard } from '../auth/guards/jwt-auth.guard';

@Controller('disputes')
export class DisputesController {
  constructor(private disputesService: DisputesService) {}

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post()
  create(@Request() req, @Body() dto: CreateDisputeDto) {
    return this.disputesService.create(req.user.id, dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get()
  findAll(@Request() req) {
    if (req.user.role === 'ADMIN') {
      return this.disputesService.findAll();
    }
    return this.disputesService.findByUser(req.user.id);
  }

  @Get(':id')
  findOne(@Param('id') id: string) {
    return this.disputesService.findOne(id);
  }

  @Get('project/:projectId')
  findByProject(@Param('projectId') projectId: string) {
    return this.disputesService.findByProject(projectId);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Put(':id/status')
  updateStatus(@Param('id') id: string, @Body('status') status: string, @Request() req) {
    return this.disputesService.updateStatus(id, req.user.id, status);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post(':id/resolve')
  resolve(@Param('id') id: string, @Request() req, @Body() dto: ResolveDisputeDto) {
    return this.disputesService.resolve(id, req.user.id, dto);
  }

  @Get('stats/overview')
  getStatistics() {
    return this.disputesService.getStatistics();
  }
}

📁 Archivo 81: backend/src/modules/prometeo/prometeo.service.ts
typescript
import { Injectable } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrismaService } from '../../prisma/prisma.service';
import { AnalyzeProjectDto, GenerateProposalDto } from './dto/prometeo.dto';

@Injectable()
export class PrometeoService {
  constructor(private prisma: PrismaService) {}

  async analyzeProject(projectId: string, dto: AnalyzeProjectDto) {
    // Simulación de análisis de IA
    // En producción, esto llamaría a OpenAI o un modelo propio
    
    const analysis = {
      riskScore: Math.random() * 100,
      estimatedDuration: dto.estimatedDuration || 30,
      recommendedBudget: dto.budget || 50000,
      potentialIssues: [
        'Verificar disponibilidad de materiales',
        'Coordinar accesos al sitio',
      ],
      recommendations: [
        'Solicitar múltiples cotizaciones',
        'Establecer hitos claros',
      ],
      marketComparison: {
        avgPrice: 45000,
        minPrice: 35000,
        maxPrice: 65000,
      },
    };

    // Guardar análisis en la base de datos
    await this.prisma.prometeoAnalysis.upsert({
      where: { projectId },
      update: {
        analysis: analysis as any,
        riskScore: analysis.riskScore,
        costEstimate: analysis.recommendedBudget,
        durationEstimate: analysis.estimatedDuration,
      },
      create: {
        projectId,
        analysis: analysis as any,
        riskScore: analysis.riskScore,
        costEstimate: analysis.recommendedBudget,
        durationEstimate: analysis.estimatedDuration,
      },
    });

    return analysis;
  }

  async generateProposal(dto: GenerateProposalDto) {
    // Simulación de generación de propuesta con IA
    const proposal = {
      summary: `Propuesta profesional para ${dto.projectType}`,
      description: `Basado en el análisis del proyecto, se recomienda un enfoque estructurado...`,
      estimatedBudget: dto.budget || 50000,
      estimatedDuration: dto.duration || 30,
      milestones: [
        { name: 'Inicio y planificación', percentage: 10 },
        { name: 'Preparación del sitio', percentage: 15 },
        { name: 'Ejecución principal', percentage: 50 },
        { name: 'Acabados y detalles', percentage: 15 },
        { name: 'Entrega y cierre', percentage: 10 },
      ],
      materials: [
        { name: 'Materiales principales', estimatedCost: 20000 },
        { name: 'Mano de obra', estimatedCost: 25000 },
        { name: 'Imprevistos (10%)', estimatedCost: 5000 },
      ],
      recommendations: [
        'Realizar reunión semanal de seguimiento',
        'Documentar cada hito con evidencias fotográficas',
      ],
    };

    return proposal;
  }

  async verifyEvidence(evidenceId: string) {
    const evidence = await this.prisma.evidence.findUnique({
      where: { id: evidenceId },
    });

    if (!evidence) {
      return { verified: false, reason: 'Evidencia no encontrada' };
    }

    // Simulación de verificación con IA
    // En producción, usaría visión computacional
    const verification = {
      verified: true,
      confidence: 0.92,
      analysis: 'La imagen parece ser auténtica y relevante para el proyecto',
      detectedObjects: ['pared', 'pintura', 'herramientas'],
    };

    if (verification.verified && !evidence.verifiedAt) {
      await this.prisma.evidence.update({
        where: { id: evidenceId },
        data: { verifiedAt: new Date() },
      });
    }

    return verification;
  }

  async assistDispute(disputeId: string) {
    const dispute = await this.prisma.dispute.findUnique({
      where: { id: disputeId },
      include: {
        project: {
          include: {
            milestones: { include: { evidence: true } },
            messages: { orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' }, take: 50 },
          },
        },
      },
    });

    if (!dispute) {
      return { error: 'Disputa no encontrada' };
    }

    // Simulación de análisis de disputa con IA
    const analysis = {
      summary: 'Análisis automatizado de la disputa',
      keyPoints: [
        'El cliente reporta que el trabajo no cumple con lo acordado',
        'El profesional ha subido evidencias del avance',
      ],
      recommendation: 'Se sugiere revisar las evidencias del último hito y programar una reunión de conciliación',
      suggestedResolution: 'Liberación parcial del pago (50%) más trabajo correctivo',
    };

    return analysis;
  }

  async suggestContract(projectId: string) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({
      where: { id: projectId },
      include: {
        client: true,
        milestones: true,
      },
    });

    if (!project) {
      return { error: 'Proyecto no encontrado' };
    }

    // Generar contrato sugerido por IA
    const contract = {
      title: `Contrato de Servicios - ${project.title}`,
      parties: {
        client: project.client.name,
        professional: '[Nombre del profesional]',
      },
      scope: project.description,
      amount: project.presupuesto || 0,
      milestones: project.milestones.map(m => ({
        description: m.title,
        amount: m.amount,
        dueDate: m.dueDate,
      })),
      terms: [
        'El pago se libera por hito aprobado',
        'Se requiere evidencia fotográfica de cada etapa',
        'Cualquier cambio en el alcance debe ser acordado por escrito',
      ],
      cancellationPolicy: 'En caso de cancelación, se cobrará el porcentaje de avance más 15% por administrativos',
    };

    return contract;
  }

  async generateReport(projectId: string) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({
      where: { id: projectId },
      include: {
        milestones: { include: { evidence: true } },
        messages: true,
      },
    });

    if (!project) {
      return { error: 'Proyecto no encontrado' };
    }

    const report = {
      projectSummary: {
        title: project.title,
        status: project.status,
        startDate: project.createdAt,
        completionRate: project.milestones.filter(m => m.status === 'APPROVED').length / project.milestones.length * 100,
      },
      milestones: project.milestones.map(m => ({
        name: m.title,
        status: m.status,
        completedAt: m.completedAt,
        evidenceCount: m.evidence?.length || 0,
      })),
      communication: {
        totalMessages: project.messages.length,
        averageResponseTime: '2.5 horas',
      },
      recommendations: [
        'Finalizar los hitos pendientes',
        'Solicitar feedback al cliente',
      ],
      generatedAt: new Date(),
    };

    return report;
  }

  async getProjectRecommendations(projectId: string) {
    const project = await this.prisma.project.findUnique({
      where: { id: projectId },
      include: {
        milestones: true,
        prometeoAnalysis: true,
      },
    });

    if (!project) {
      return { error: 'Proyecto no encontrado' };
    }

    const recommendations = {
      timeline: [
        'Revisar hitos próximos a vencer',
        'Programar reunión de seguimiento',
      ],
      budget: [
        'Monitorear gastos vs presupuesto',
        'Considerar reserva para imprevistos',
      ],
      quality: [
        'Solicitar evidencias frecuentes',
        'Realizar inspecciones periódicas',
      ],
      risk: project.prometeoAnalysis?.riskScore > 70 
        ? ['Alto riesgo detectado - Tomar acciones correctivas'] 
        : ['Riesgo bajo - Continuar con el plan actual'],
    };

    return recommendations;
  }
}
📁 Archivo 82: backend/src/modules/prometeo/prometeo.controller.ts
typescript
import { Controller, Post, Get, Body, Param, UseGuards, Request } from '@nestjs/common';
import { PrometeoService } from './prometeo.service';
import { AnalyzeProjectDto, GenerateProposalDto } from './dto/prometeo.dto';
import { JwtAuthGuard } from '../auth/guards/jwt-auth.guard';

@Controller('prometeo')
export class PrometeoController {
  constructor(private prometeoService: PrometeoService) {}

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post('analyze/:projectId')
  analyzeProject(@Param('projectId') projectId: string, @Body() dto: AnalyzeProjectDto) {
    return this.prometeoService.analyzeProject(projectId, dto);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post('generate-proposal')
  generateProposal(@Body() dto: GenerateProposalDto) {
    return this.prometeoService.generateProposal(dto);
  }

  @Post('verify-evidence/:evidenceId')
  verifyEvidence(@Param('evidenceId') evidenceId: string) {
    return this.prometeoService.verifyEvidence(evidenceId);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post('assist-dispute/:disputeId')
  assistDispute(@Param('disputeId') disputeId: string) {
    return this.prometeoService.assistDispute(disputeId);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Post('suggest-contract/:projectId')
  suggestContract(@Param('projectId') projectId: string) {
    return this.prometeoService.suggestContract(projectId);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get('report/:projectId')
  generateReport(@Param('projectId') projectId: string) {
    return this.prometeoService.generateReport(projectId);
  }

  @UseGuards(JwtAuthGuard)
  @Get('recommendations/:projectId')
  getRecommendations(@Param('projectId') projectId: string) {
    return this.prometeoService.getProjectRecommendations(projectId);
  }
}
📁 Archivo 83: backend/src/modules/prometeo/dto/prometeo.dto.ts
typescript
import { IsString, IsOptional, IsNumber, IsArray } from 'class-validator';

export class AnalyzeProjectDto {
  @IsOptional()
  @IsNumber()
  estimatedDuration?: number;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsNumber()
  budget?: number;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsArray()
  @IsString({ each: true })
  requirements?: string[];
}

export class GenerateProposalDto {
  @IsString()
  projectType: string;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsNumber()
  budget?: number;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsNumber()
  duration?: number;

  @IsOptional()
  @IsString()
  description?: string;
}
